# AUDIT

> Open audit findings. `/iterate` reads the Pending section
> and ships the highest-scoring item per tick. Score formula:
> `impact × ease / 10`, then apply the bias multiplier from
> the header (if present) for the matching category.
>
> Categories: `bug`, `perf`, `a11y`, `seo`, `content-gaps`,
> `data`, `docs`, `mod`, `spoiler`, `other`.

<!-- Bias mechanism — set via /oversight to direct iterate's focus.
     Format:
       > Bias: <category> (set 2026-MM-DD via oversight, valid for N ticks)
     Multiplies findings of <category> by 1.5x for ranking. -->

<!-- No active bias. The content-gaps bias (set 2026-06-11) was
     cleared via oversight 2026-06-14 — /iterate now ranks purely
     by impact × ease. Show-expansion content rows carry their own
     score and dispatch through /ship-content (march Step 3b.5),
     so they do not need a bias thumb on the scale. -->

- [ ] [HIGH] Nightly e2e-full breadth crawl went red 2026-07-06T23:27Z (run 28830277979) — NOT a test regression, a duration-ceiling breach: all 6,409 checks that completed passed; the "Exhaustive e2e crawl (E2E_FULL=1)" step hit `.github/workflows/e2e-full.yml`'s hard `timeout-minutes: 50` with only 164 of 6,573 tests remaining (97.5% complete). The crawl runs Playwright single-worker (`Running 6573 tests using 1 worker`, ~460ms/test), so wall-clock scales linearly with total page count, which scales with the content saga's own perpetual mandate (53 shows / 700 seasons as of this filing and climbing). This will recur on a predictable schedule as the catalog keeps growing — it is not a one-off flake. **BLOCKED FROM CLOUD**: the fix (raise `timeout-minutes` on that step from 50 to ~75, job-level budget has headroom) requires editing `.github/workflows/e2e-full.yml`, which the cloud loop's `ACTIONS_PAT` cannot push (lacks `workflows` OAuth scope) — identical blocker to the Supabase CLI pin row below (issue #416/#480). Do not re-attempt from cloud; needs a local/`/oversight` session, ideally bundled with the Supabase CLI pin since both are one-line diffs to the same file family blocked by the same permission gap. Filed as `PHASE_CANDIDATES.md` candidate #26 (2026-07-07 digest) with the full scope sketch. (category: engineering, source: self, score: 3.5 — impact 5 × ease 7) — filed 2026-07-03 during the nexus readopt — issue: #449 — RESOLVED: `resolveCandidates` in `scripts/lib/check-test-colocation.mjs` unconditionally prepended a leading `/` when rebuilding the resolved path from segments, which is correct for POSIX-rooted dirs but produces `/Z:/...` (never matching the real `Z:/...`) for Windows drive-rooted dirs. Added a drive-letter-root check that skips the prepend in that case, plus colocated tests pinning both path shapes.

Fixing it hit a numbering snag: external sources (Wikipedia's List of Naked and Afraid episodes, epguides) put main-series S13 premiering Aug 1 2021 (not 2022) and S16 premiering Oct 15 2023 (not 2024) — our internal season numbers are offset by one from the real-world main-series numbering (S12 and S15 do match). This may mean our catalog folds in an XL/spinoff season somewhere, or has an off-by-one from an early miscount — needs an editorial call on which numbering convention this catalog intends before any date gets corrected, since blindly applying the external dates would silently reassign which real-world season maps to which of our canonical_position slots. - [x] [MED] `{yearsWord}` tagline/card_tagline token always substitutes a lowercase spelled-out number (`numberToWords()` in `src/lib/show-tenure.ts`), which rendered a lowercase word opening a new sentence wherever a tagline places the token right after a period — the exact defect CRITIQUE passes 53/58/66 flagged independently as one-off content typos on below-deck-mediterranean, below-deck-sailing-yacht, dancing-with-the-stars, and masked-singer, without anyone spotting the shared root cause. A catalog-wide grep for the token found the same live bug on 4 more shows those passes hadn't reached (below-deck-down-under, americas-got-talent, americas-next-top-model, the-apprentice) — 8 shows total, all fixed by one render-layer change instead of 8 separate content edits. (category: bug, source: self, score: 5.6 — impact 7 × ease 8) — filed 2026-07-04 during iterate audit — issue: #457 — RESOLVED: `renderShowTaglineTokens` now capitalizes the substituted `{yearsWord}` only when it opens the string or follows sentence-ending punctuation (`.`/`!`/`?` + whitespace); mid-sentence uses (the common case) are untouched. `{years}` (digits) is unaffected — no case to fix. Pinning tests added in `src/lib/__tests__/show-tenure.test.ts` (start-of-string, after each punctuation mark, mid-sentence negative case, `{years}` negative case) and two existing synthetic test fixtures updated to reflect the corrected (and intentional) capitalization. No content files touched — the fix is purely in the shared render path, so all 8 affected shows self-heal without an editorial pass.

- [x] [HIGH] [user-issue #402] Cloud verify-gate e2e leg is structurally red because the Supabase `service_role` has only `TRUNCATE / REFERENCES / TRIGGER` on every phase-11/12/13 `public.*` table (`users`, `sessions`, `votes`, `comments`, `flags`, `mod_actions`, `ai_decisions`, `rank_snapshots`) — no `SELECT / INSERT / UPDATE / DELETE`. Every authed-write spec (`comment-backend`, `comment-read`, `community-page`, `ranking-api`, `user-profile`, `vote-state-pill`) trips on `POST /api/vote` or `POST /api/comment` returning 500 with `{"ok":false,"error":"auth_resolve_failed","detail":"upsertUser: permission denied for table users"}`. RLS bypass on `service_role` doesn't override missing GRANTs at the postgres layer. Root cause: migrations run as the `postgres` role, whose `pg_default_acl` in schema `public` does NOT include grants to `anon / authenticated / service_role` — only objects created by `supabase_admin` get the auto-grants the Supabase API roles need. Cloud loop has been hitting this since ~2026-06-11 10:06Z; supabase CLI 2.106.0 in this run. (category: data, source: triage, score: 7.2 — impact 9 × ease 8) — e772dfc — issue: #402 — RESOLVED this commit: took fix shape (a) — added `supabase/migrations/20260611000001_grant_api_roles.sql` that explicitly grants `SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE` on the eight in-scope tables (`users`, `sessions`, `votes`, `comments`, `flags`, `ai_decisions`, `mod_actions`, `rank_snapshots`) to `anon, authenticated, service_role`. The migration matches the standard Supabase pattern for tables created by `supabase_admin`; the existing RLS policies in migrations 000001/000003/000004/000007/000008/000009/000013/000015 continue to gate row-level access for anon and authenticated, and service_role bypasses RLS as before — GRANTs are the postgres ACL layer, RLS is the row filter, both must permit. Belt-and-braces: also (b) `grant usage, select on all sequences in schema public` (no current bigserial columns; defends future ones), and (c) `alter default privileges for role postgres in schema public grant ... on tables` + `... on sequences` so any future `create table` migration applied by `postgres` inherits the GRANTs automatically and a regression cannot silently re-ship locked tables. Migration is idempotent on `db reset`. Proof of fix: the same red e2e specs went green — leg 3 ran 1362 passed (was 13 failed before the migration on this very tick). Verify gate green all three legs: leg1 tokens + typecheck + no-raw-img + colocation + 193 unit files / 2684 tests + script + content:check (13 shows / 298 seasons / 13 canons / 12 themes / 3 legal docs); leg2 build; leg3 1362 e2e (incl. the 13 previously-failing authed-write specs). Closes #402.

- [x] [HIGH] `pnpm verify` is structurally broken on every Windows checkout — two independent environment bugs, both verified 2026-06-11 by /oversight on a clean main working tree and both invisible to the Linux-only cloud loop + Vercel: (1) the phase-42 colocation gate exits 1 with `found 308 testless source module(s)` (every module flagged, including the `__tests__/*.test.*` files themselves) because `scripts/check-test-colocation.mjs` walks with `node:path` `join` — backslash separators on win32 — but filters test files with the POSIX literal `'/__tests__/'` (line 57) and the pure lib `scripts/lib/check-test-colocation.mjs` splits/joins on `'/'` in `expectedTestPaths`/`resolveCandidates`; fix by normalizing walked paths to forward slashes at the CLI boundary before they reach the lib, and pin a regression test feeding backslash paths; (2) `src/content/__tests__/hvv-take-shape-opener-echo.test.ts` fails 3/7 on Windows (`expected '' to match …` — its TAKE/SHAPE section extraction returns empty) on both vitest 3.2.4 and 3.2.6, the CRLF-checkout class: the extraction regex anchors on `\n` while a default `core.autocrlf` checkout delivers CRLF in `content/shows/survivor/seasons/20-heroes-vs-villains.md`; normalize `\r\n` to `\n` before matching (the sibling echo tests pass on Windows — mirror their approach). Until both land, the local verify gate cannot go green on the user's machine, which silently blocks every local shipping skill. The lib remains POSIX-only — paths reach it already in `/`-separated form, so `expectedTestPaths` / `resolveCandidates` (which split/join on `'/'`) work uniformly across platforms. **(2)** `src/content/__tests__/hvv-take-shape-opener-echo.test.ts` gained a `readRaw()` helper that normalizes `\r\n` → `\n` once before either match runs; `readBody()` + `readPull()` thread through it. - [x] [MED] `/` (the home page) emits zero JSON-LD — the only top-level public surface in the product without machine-readable structured data, the bare spot a `WebSite`-type signal is meant to fill. Every other page family emits its own type-specific JSON-LD via `jsonLdScriptProps`: show pages emit `CollectionPage` + `ItemList` + `BreadcrumbList` (`src/app/shows/[show]/page.tsx`), season pages emit `Article` + `BreadcrumbList` (`src/app/shows/[show]/season/[slug]/page.tsx`), `/shows` emits `ItemList`, `/themes` + `/themes/[theme]` emit `CollectionPage`/`ItemList`, `/about` emits `FAQPage`, `/u/[handle]` emits `ProfilePage`. `src/app/(default)/page.tsx:36-45` defines `generateMetadata` (title, description, canonical, OG, RSS discovery) but the render function emits no `<script type="application/ld+json">` at all — `grep -rn '@type.*WebSite\\|@type.*Organization' src/ content/` returns zero matches. The brand's root surface is the canonical place to declare the publisher in a way crawlers can read; absent that, Google has to infer the publisher from OG tags alone (less reliable, weaker for brand panels in SERPs). schema.org's `WebSite` is the documented type for this — declared once on the home page, name + description + url. Do **not** include a `SearchAction` / `potentialAction.SearchAction` block — `/search` is not a real route in the product (the header's `SearchTrigger` replaced a legacy `/search` link, see `src/components/search/SearchTrigger.tsx:5`); declaring a SearchAction whose `urlTemplate` 404s would mislead crawlers and is worse than emitting nothing. Fix: (a) extend `buildJsonLd` in `src/lib/seo.ts` with a new `WebSite` arm (`name: siteConfig.name`, `description`, `url: canonicalUrl('/')` — keep the existing tagged-union shape; no SearchAction); (b) call it from `src/app/(default)/page.tsx`, render `<script {...jsonLdScriptProps({ id: 'ld-website', data: ld })} />` inside the page tree, mirroring `/about`'s FAQ pattern; (c) extend `src/lib/__tests__/seo.test.ts` (`buildJsonLd` cases) with a `WebSite` case pinning `@type`/`name`/`description`/`url`; (d) extend `src/app/(default)/__tests__/page.test.tsx` with a "home emits a WebSite JSON-LD script on render" case asserting the parsed `@type === 'WebSite'`, the `url` is the home canonical, and there is no `potentialAction` key (negative pin against accidentally adding a SearchAction). No URL/schema/route change. (category: seo, source: self, score: 4.8 — impact 6 × ease 8) — 8213fc1 — issue: #286 — RESOLVED 8213fc1: took the row's full path. `src/lib/seo.ts` gained a new `WebSite` arm on the `buildJsonLd` tagged-union (`name` / `description` / `path` → `canonicalUrl(path)`); the header comment on the new arm names the documented decision to omit `potentialAction` (no `/search` route exists in the product — the header's `SearchTrigger` replaced a legacy `/search` link, declaring a SearchAction whose urlTemplate 404s would mislead crawlers). `src/app/(default)/page.tsx` imports `buildJsonLd` + `jsonLdScriptProps`, builds a `WebSite` payload (`name: 'tiered.tv'`, `description: HOME_DESCRIPTION`, `path: '/'`) inside the render function, and emits `<script {...jsonLdScriptProps({ id: 'ld-website', data: websiteLd })} />` as the first child of the page tree — mirroring `/about`'s FAQ pattern. `src/lib/__tests__/seo.test.ts` gained a `WebSite` case pinning the full `@context`/`@type`/`name`/`description`/`url` shape (URL canonicalised to `BASE/`) plus an `expect(jsonLd).not.toHaveProperty('potentialAction')` negative pin. `src/app/(default)/__tests__/page.test.tsx` gained two new cases in a fresh describe block: (1) the page renders `<script id="ld-website" type="application/ld+json">`, the JSON parses to `@context: schema.org` + `@type: WebSite` + `name: tiered.tv` + a non-empty description + `url: https://tiered.tv/`; (2) bidirectional negative pin — the parsed payload has no `potentialAction` key AND the raw script textContent contains no literal `/SearchAction/i` (so a future edit that accidentally adds the type cannot regress without tripping the unit gate). The negative-pin comment cross-references the in-source rationale and tells a future maintainer how to update both gates in lockstep if a real `/search` page ever ships alongside a SearchAction. - [x] [MED] Voice break on the season-page vote eyebrow: the `signed-in-no-vote` head meta literal in `src/components/composition/VoteRowHead.tsx:35` reads `cast yours` (rendered uppercase by CSS) — a possessive-elision fragment that critique pass-22 surveyed as the only clever-fragment CTA on the entire authed walk while every sibling site-wide CTA stays plain (`Browse all shows`, `Start with Survivor`, `Go to Survivor`, `How it works`, `read the list`, `Sign out`). Plan/bearings's voice cue says `plain sentences over clever ones`; the elision relies on the reader filling in "vote" from the parent title's `Your vote`, while the surrounding helper text already says `Does this belong in the community top 10?` plainly. Same class as the pass-19 #242 + pass-20 community-pane "recompute" sweeps — page knows how to talk plainly elsewhere, this one literal is the outlier. Fix: swap the literal to `cast vote` (single plain imperative; CSS continues to render `CAST VOTE` uppercase), extend the colocated `VoteRowHead.test.tsx` signed-in-no-vote assertion to the new copy + add a negative regex pin against `/cast yours/i` so a regression back to the elision form fails at unit time, update the e2e `vote-state-pill.spec.ts:113` assertion + the source/test/CSS comments referencing the prior literal. None of its contracts are pinned by a hermetic e2e walk (the walk reads rendered pages, not the `Metadata`-object construction nor the inline bootstrap-script string): (1) **`metadata` export** (`src/app/layout.tsx:7-39`) — `metadataBase = new URL(siteConfig.baseUrl)` (every relative canonical/OG URL resolves against it; a regression hardcoding a different base or dropping the URL wrapper breaks all of them), `title.default` (the full brand promise) + `title.template` (`'%s — tiered.tv'`, applied to every child route's `<title>` — a regression dropping it strips the brand suffix site-wide), `description` (spoiler-free + the two-rankings frame), `applicationName`, the global RSS `application/rss+xml` alternate at `/feed.xml` (feed-reader auto-discovery, dark to e2e — the walk fetches `/feed.xml` directly, never greps the `<head>` alternate), the favicon set SVG-first with the `.ico` universal fallback + apple-touch-icon (order is load-bearing for which asset a browser picks). (2) **`viewport` export** (`src/app/layout.tsx:41-45`) — `themeColor = '#0E0B08'` (brand paper, the mobile browser-chrome tint), `width = 'device-width'`, `initialScale = 1`. (3) **No-flicker theme bootstrap** (`src/app/layout.tsx:47,52-54`) — a synchronous IIFE reading `localStorage.getItem('tiered_theme')`, gating on `'light'||'dark'`, applying `documentElement.dataset.theme`, wrapped in `try/catch` so a blocked localStorage (private mode) can't throw before first paint. Never fires during the e2e walk (no theme set), so the branch is entirely dark to it; a regression dropping the gate (applies any junk value, breaking the CSS theme cascade) or the try/catch (throws + blocks paint in private mode) would ship unnoticed. (4) **`<html>`/`<body>` shell** (`src/app/layout.tsx:50-62`) — `<html lang="en" suppressHydrationWarning>` (the suppress flag is required because the bootstrap mutates `dataset.theme` before hydration), the `<body className="flex min-h-dvh flex-col">` sticky-footer shell every page depends on, children rendered first with both analytics beacons trailing (analytics must not wrap content). - [x] [MED] `src/app/(default)/sign-in/page.tsx` ships without a colocated test — the next-by-impact testless `src/app/` route after the #131–#193 drain pinned every `src/app/api/` route handler plus `src/middleware.ts`, `src/app/sitemap.ts`, `src/app/robots.ts`, `src/app/feed.xml/route.ts`, `src/app/feed/[slug]/route.ts`, every `*/opengraph-image.tsx` variant, the root `src/app/opengraph-image.tsx`, and the phase-33 page-level `permanentRedirect` pair (canon #180 + community #193). `/sign-in` is the magic-link entry point — the only auth-flow page in the product. 70 lines composing five behaviors none of which a hermetic e2e walk pins from the outside (the e2e walk needs an anon session, hits `/sign-in`, asserts the form is reachable; it cannot pin the signed-in redirect branch nor `noIndex` nor the `encodeURIComponent` discipline on the loginHref query string): (1) **Segment-config export** (`src/app/(default)/sign-in/page.tsx:7`) — `dynamic = 'force-dynamic'` — the route reads per-viewer auth state; baking it static would serve one viewer's session to everyone. (2) **`generateMetadata` + `noIndex` discipline** (`src/app/(default)/sign-in/page.tsx:9-16`) — title `'Sign in'`, description names magic link by email, path `/sign-in`, `noIndex: true`. The `noIndex` is load-bearing: sign-in pages have zero search value, indexing them dilutes the home's PageRank and produces noisy SERP entries. A regression dropping `noIndex` would let Googlebot index the sign-in flow — the SEO equivalent of indexing `/api/`. (3) **Signed-in redirect branch** (`src/app/(default)/sign-in/page.tsx:23-29`) — when `auth0.getSession()` returns a user, `redirect(returnTo)` fires. The redirect target is the bare returnTo, NOT the loginHref (would loop the magic-link flow); `next/navigation.redirect` (302) is appropriate for a session-scoped bounce, not `permanentRedirect`. (4) **`returnTo` default + URL encoding** (`src/app/(default)/sign-in/page.tsx:24-25,31`) — `returnTo = params.return ?? '/'` (the default is home, not undefined which would yield `?returnTo=undefined`). `loginHref = '/auth/login?returnTo=${encodeURIComponent(returnTo)}'` — the `encodeURIComponent` is load-bearing: a regression to raw interpolation would corrupt the query string on any returnTo containing `&`, `?`, `=`, `%`, or unicode (e.g. `/shows/survivor?view=community` would lose the `view=community` slice on the Auth0 round-trip). (5) **Form + Link contract** (`src/app/(default)/sign-in/page.tsx:48-63`) — form `action={loginHref}` + `method="get"`; the Continue Link `href={loginHref}` + `prefetch={false}` (the auth flow must not prefetch — it would consume the magic link); the three data-testids (`sign-in-page` / `sign-in-form` / `sign-in-continue`) are the hooks the e2e auth spec keys off. - [x] [MED] `src/app/shows/[show]/community/page.tsx` ships without a colocated test — the second half of the phase-33 page-level `permanentRedirect` pair (canon was the first, pinned in #180 / `1ce476e`). The standalone Community Rank page was consolidated into the show page, so this route 308s every legacy `/shows/<slug>/community` URL into the consolidated show page on the community pane via `/shows/<slug>?view=community`. 19 lines composing three behaviors none of which a hermetic e2e walk pins from the outside (e2e walks that the redirect lands; it cannot pin that the redirect uses 308 vs 302 nor that a future regression dropped the `?view=community` query): (1) **`generateStaticParams`** (`src/app/shows/[show]/community/page.tsx:13-15`) — returns one row per `getAllShows()` show with the bracket-segment-shaped key `{ show: <slug> }`. A regression to `{ slug: ... }` would render zero static params and the route would fall through to on-demand SSR, defeating SSG. (2) **Redirect target with REQUIRED query string** (`src/app/shows/[show]/community/page.tsx:18`) — `permanentRedirect('/shows/${params.show}?view=community')`. The query string is load-bearing here, inverse of the canon redirect: canon is the default pane on the consolidated show page, but community needs the explicit `?view=community` flag. A regression dropping the query would land every legacy community URL on the canon pane and silently bleed community-page SEO authority onto the wrong destination; appending a trailing slash before the `?` would violate the locked `/shows/<slug>` URL contract. (3) **Redirect mechanism** (`src/app/shows/[show]/community/page.tsx:18`) — `permanentRedirect` (308) rather than `redirect` (302). The behavioral difference is invisible to a Playwright follow-redirect walk (both land on the same page), but search engines treat them very differently: 308 transfers PageRank to the new URL, 302 does not. A regression `permanentRedirect` → `redirect` would silently drain accumulated SEO authority off the `/shows/<slug>/community` URL family. (2) **ImageResponse construction** (`src/app/opengraph-image.tsx:8-52`) — the route directly constructs a `new ImageResponse(jsx, {...size})` and returns it (no fan-out, no double-render); a regression that wrapped the response or constructed multiple instances per call would break the build's static OG image pipeline. (3) **Brand text content** (`src/app/opengraph-image.tsx:25,35,45`) — three rendered text spans: `"tiered.tv"` (wordmark), `"the seasons, ranked."` (promise-first), `"no spoilers."` (promise-second), rendered in that document order — splitting the promise across two lines is intentional editorial register (beat-pause between offer and constraint). (4) **Brand palette** (`src/app/opengraph-image.tsx:14,20,24,31,41`) — five hand-rolled hex values: paper `#0E0B08`, inherited ink `#F2EADB`, wordmark gold `#E8B65A`, bright ink `#D8CFBE` (offer line), muted ink `#9D9485` (constraint line) — the root OG is brand-anchored not show-anchored, so the palette is hardcoded here rather than threaded from `--show-*` tokens; a regression that drifted any of the five hexes would visually corrupt the share card on every default-OG share. The card's layout shape — flex column, items flex-start, content justified center, 140px wordmark + 56px couplet — is the editorial-block register; a regression to `alignItems: 'center'` would re-cast the brand mark as a stamp and break the editorial voice. - [x] [MED] `src/app/shows/[show]/season/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx` ships without a colocated test — the next-by-impact testless `src/app/` route after the 13-tick #131–#146 drain pinned every `src/app/api/` route handler (#131 `/api/auth/me`, #132 `/api/internal/recompute`, #134 `/api/vote`, #135 `/api/comment`, #136 `/api/comments`, #137 `/api/ranking/[show]`, #140 `/api/flag`, #141 `/api/mod/action`) plus `src/middleware.ts` (#142), `src/app/sitemap.ts` (#143), `src/app/robots.ts` (#144), `src/app/feed.xml/route.ts` (#145), and `src/app/feed/[slug]/route.ts` (#146). `app/shows/[show]/season/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx` is the per-season social-share card every link to `/shows/<show>/season/<slug>` hits from Slack, iMessage, Twitter, Facebook, etc — the discovery surface that drives traffic for **298 season slugs** across the catalog. 46 lines composing six behaviors none of which a hermetic e2e walk pins from the outside (e2e walks the OG URL is reachable, not the pixel content): (1) **Two `notFound()` branches** (`src/app/shows/[show]/season/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx:24,26`) — unknown show → `notFound()`; known show + unknown season → `notFound()`. A regression that fell through with `show: undefined` would 500 on the `show.palette` read; a regression that 200'd on an unknown season would render an empty card with a missing title. (2) **`padRank` helper** (`src/app/shows/[show]/season/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx:12-15`) — `null/undefined → ''`, single-digit `n` → `#0n`, two-digit `n` → `#nn`, three-digit `n` → `#nnn`. A regression to non-padded would emit `#1` instead of `#01` on every top-of-canon share card; a regression to fixed-width pad would emit `#001` and break the visual rhythm. (3) **Canon-rank lookup + three-step fallback chain** (`src/app/shows/[show]/season/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx:28-30`) — `getCanon(showSlug)?.entries.find(e => e.season === season.number)?.rank ?? season.canonical_position ?? null`. The chain pins four branches: canon-file rank wins over `canonical_position`; null canon falls back to `season.canonical_position`; canon-file with no matching entry falls back to `season.canonical_position`; neither set → null. The lookup matches on `season.number` (not title / slug) — a regression matching on the wrong field would label every season `#01` because the top-ranked season is always at index 0. (4) **Eyebrow conditional** (`src/app/shows/[show]/season/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx:31-33`) — truthy canonRank → `"Tiers / ${show.name} · Editor's Canon ${padRank(rank)}"`; falsy → `"Tiers / ${show.name} · Season ${season.number}"`. The two strings are the literal copy every social card surfaces in the eyebrow row. (5) **Blurb fallback chain** (`src/app/shows/[show]/season/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx:38-39`) — `season.lede ?? season.tag ?? \`${show.name}, season ${season.number}.\``. The lede is the curator's hand-authored season opener — preferring it over `tag` (a short marketing-style label) is load-bearing for editorial voice; a regression swapping the order would surface "all-stars" or "second chances" where "The all-stars season the format spent twenty years earning." should appear. The composed fallback uses `show.name` (not the URL slug — kebab slugs read wrong as copy). (6) **Palette pass-through + segment-config exports** (`src/app/shows/[show]/season/[slug]/opengraph-image.tsx:5-8,40-44`) — `show.palette.{paper,ink,primary}` extracted into the `buildOgImage({palette})` argument (no spread of the whole palette object, so future palette siblings don't pollute the OG factory); the four Next-required segment-config exports (`runtime = 'nodejs'`, `alt`, `size: {width: 1200, height: 630}`, `contentType = 'image/png'`). The `runtime = 'nodejs'` is load-bearing — the route reads from the content layer (file-system loaders) so a regression to `'edge'` (the root `/opengraph-image.tsx` shape) would 500 every season OG card at build time. The underlying `buildOgImage` template is exhaustively tested in `src/lib/og/__tests__/template.test.tsx` (mocked `next/og` ImageResponse, captured tree walk for tokens); the route handler's own contracts — eyebrow conditional, padRank, blurb fallback chain, two notFound branches, palette extraction, segment-config exports — are dark to e2e. - [x] [MED] `src/app/robots.ts` ships without a colocated test — the next-by-impact testless `src/app/` route after the 10-tick #131–#143 drain pinned every `src/app/api/` route handler plus `src/middleware.ts` (#142) and `src/app/sitemap.ts` (#143). `app/robots.ts` is the Next.js `MetadataRoute.Robots` producer that **every search engine** reads at `/robots.txt` — the single declarative surface that tells crawlers what they may and may not index across tiered.tv. 16 lines composing four behaviors none of which a hermetic e2e walk pins from the outside: (1) **disallow list** (`src/app/robots.ts:10`) — `['/api/', '/mod', '/sign-in']`. The trailing slash on `/api/` is load-bearing — `/api` (no slash) would block `/apiary`, `/api-docs`, and any future `/api`-prefixed page family; the bare `/mod` correctly blocks `/mod` AND `/mod/*` (the queue surface where pending comments would expose author handles + flagged content); `/sign-in` blocks the Auth0 sign-in flow, a no-content redirect surface that has zero search value. Drop any one path from this list and a private surface gets indexed — the mod-queue exposure is the loudest. (2) **`userAgent: '*'` + `allow: '/'`** — open to all crawlers on every path except the disallow set; a regression that tightened `allow` would silently de-index the entire site. (3) **`sitemap: canonicalUrl('/sitemap.xml')`** — points crawlers to the absolute sitemap URL `https://tiered.tv/sitemap.xml`; a regression returning the raw path would emit a relative URL crawlers cannot follow. (4) **`host: siteConfig.baseUrl`** — the bare baseUrl `'https://tiered.tv'` (NOT canonicalUrl-wrapped — different shape from `sitemap`); a regression that ran `canonicalUrl` here would append a trailing slash `'https://tiered.tv/'` and break Yandex's strict `Host:` directive parser. The `host` vs `sitemap` shape distinction is the kind of detail typecheck cannot enforce (both are strings) and e2e cannot exercise (Next.js serializes the same way), so a unit test is the only structural defense. (category: tests, source: self, score: 7.2) — RESOLVED this commit (#144): added `src/app/__tests__/robots.test.ts` with 17 cases across 5 describes, modeled on the #143 sitemap precedent — `@/lib/seo` left **real** so a regression in `canonicalUrl`'s trailing-slash discipline or `siteConfig.baseUrl` surfaces here, not just in the helper's own test; the route has no external inputs so no mocking is needed. Top-level shape (object keys exactly `{rules, sitemap, host}`; `rules` has exactly one entry; the function is pure — repeated calls return equal output). Rule entry (`userAgent: '*'` pinned; `allow: '/'` pinned; rule keys exactly `{userAgent, allow, disallow}` — no extra keys, none missing). Disallow list (exact-order equality on `['/api/', '/mod', '/sign-in']`; the trailing slash on `/api/` defended via positive + negative assertion — `'/api/'` present AND `'/api'` absent; `/mod` and `/sign-in` membership pinned individually; over-blocking guard — `/shows`, `/themes`, `/`, `/about` each NOT in disallow). Sitemap pointer (output equals the hardcoded `'https://tiered.tv/sitemap.xml'` AND equals `canonicalUrl('/sitemap.xml')` — belt-and-braces against drift in either layer; output type is `string`, not array/object). Host directive (output equals `'https://tiered.tv'`; sourced from `siteConfig.baseUrl` directly; explicitly NOT equal to `canonicalUrl('/')` — the `host` does NOT end in `/`, pinning the shape distinction from `sitemap`). No source change. `app/robots.ts` is not a new URL (shipped phase 3 as part of the locked URL contract) so no e2e fixture row is owed — `/robots.txt` already appears in the smoke walk family via the build's static output. After this, the next-by-impact testless `src/app/` routes are `src/app/feed.xml/route.ts` (24 lines — global RSS producer with `dynamic = 'force-static'` + `revalidate = 3600` + `Content-Type: application/rss+xml; charset=utf-8` + the brand-promise title `"${siteConfig.name} — the seasons, ranked. no spoilers."`) and `src/app/feed/[slug]/route.ts` (45 lines — per-show RSS with `.xml`-suffix discipline + the unknown-show 404 branch + `generateStaticParams` enumerating every show). - [x] [MED] `src/app/sitemap.ts` ships without a colocated test — the next-by-impact testless `src/app/` route after the 9-tick #131–#142 drain pinned every `src/app/api/` route handler (#131 `/api/auth/me`, #132 `/api/internal/recompute`, #134 `/api/vote`, #135 `/api/comment`, #136 `/api/comments`, #137 `/api/ranking/[show]`, #140 `/api/flag`, #141 `/api/mod/action`) plus #142 `src/middleware.ts`. `app/sitemap.ts` is the Next.js MetadataRoute.Sitemap producer that **every search engine** reads at `/sitemap.xml` — it is the single load-bearing surface for tiered.tv's crawlable URL inventory. The route loaders (`getSitemapRoutes`, `getFeedPaths`) already have exhaustive coverage in `src/lib/__tests__/routes.test.ts` (the exclude/include rules, the `/u/[handle]` env gate, the per-show feed slug-alignment + order discipline), but the **consumer transformation** that turns those route lists into the sitemap shape was never pinned: (1) **priority differentiation** — home (`pattern === '/'`) → 1.0; non-home pages → 0.7; feed entries → 0.4; a regression keying priority off `route.path === '/'` instead of `route.pattern === '/'` keys home correctly for the current route set but breaks the pattern discipline that lets future static-route additions reuse `/` as a literal path under a different pattern; (2) **canonical-URL wrap** — every entry's `url` is `canonicalUrl(path)` (absolute against `siteConfig.baseUrl = 'https://tiered.tv'` + the trailing-slash-strip discipline `canonicalUrl` enforces); a regression that returned the raw path would emit relative URLs and fail every search engine's strict `<urlset>` parser; (3) **pages-before-feeds composition** — `return [...pages, ...feeds]` with feed entries appended after the page list; a regression to `[...feeds, ...pages]` would invert the document order most crawlers use as a freshness heuristic; (4) **changeFrequency: 'weekly'** on every entry — a regression to `'daily'` would inflate the recrawl budget (and trip rate-limits at some crawlers); (5) **single `Date` lastModified per emission** — one `const now = new Date()` shared across every entry; a regression that inlined `new Date()` per row would still typecheck but spread timestamps by a millisecond and break the "this sitemap was rendered at one instant" semantics search engines key off; (6) **the four `MetadataRoute.Sitemap` entry keys** (`url`, `lastModified`, `changeFrequency`, `priority`) — extra keys or missing keys silently break the Next.js `sitemap.xml` serializer's schema. 21 lines, two `.map()` projections, two priority constants, one shared `new Date()`, one spread-merge — every line carries an unpinned contract on the surface every Google/Bing/DuckDuckGo crawler reads, and a hermetic e2e walk against `/sitemap.xml` (which would have to inflate the response XML and assert per-entry priority/freq) is structurally a worse fit than a mock-driven unit test that drives the helpers explicitly. Page entries (one entry per `getSitemapRoutes` row → exact-URL list; every entry wrapped in `canonicalUrl` so each starts with `https://tiered.tv/`; order preserved across the `.map()` against an out-of-order helper response). Priority differentiation (home `pattern === '/'` → 1.0; the full non-home pattern surface — `/shows`, `/themes`, `/about`, `/shows/[show]`, `/shows/[show]/season/[slug]`, `/themes/[theme]` — each → 0.7 via `it.each`-shaped assertions; a synthetic `{pattern: '/shows', path: '/'}` row stays at 0.7, pinning the pattern-keyed rule against a `route.path === '/'` regression). Entry-shape contract (`changeFrequency: 'weekly'` on every page AND every feed; `lastModified` is an actual `Date` instance and the **same** `Date` across the whole emission — `(entry.lastModified as Date).getTime()` equality across pages + feeds, pinning the single-`new Date()`-per-call discipline; a second call after a 5ms `setTimeout` produces a fresh timestamp, proving the closure isn't pinned across calls; `Object.keys(entry).sort()` is exactly `['changeFrequency', 'lastModified', 'priority', 'url']` per row, pinning the four-key shape). - [x] [MED] `src/middleware.ts` ships without a colocated test — the highest-blast-radius testless surface left in `src/` after the 8-tick API-route-handler drain (#131 `/api/auth/me`, #132 `/api/internal/recompute`, #134 `/api/vote`, #135 `/api/comment`, #136 `/api/comments`, #137 `/api/ranking/[show]`, #140 `/api/flag`, #141 `/api/mod/action`) closed every `src/app/api/` route. `src/middleware.ts` is the Next.js Edge middleware that runs on every page, every API route, and every auth route per `config.matcher` (matcher excludes `_next/static`, `_next/image`, favicon, `.svg`, `.png`, `.ico`, `.json`, `.txt`). 60 lines composing three behaviors none of which a hermetic e2e walk can pin from the outside: (1) **phase-29 `/search` retirement** (`src/middleware.ts:28-33`) — `/search` 308-redirects to `/` with the query string cleared (`url.search = ''`); a regression that forwarded the query would leak stale `?q=…` into the home route, a regression to 307 would break crawl re-indexing; the early return is also load-bearing — Auth0 must NOT be invoked on the retired path (so the SDK can't accidentally redirect /search to the login flow); (2) **Auth0 SDK composition + auth-route passthrough** (`src/middleware.ts:35-41`) — `auth0.middleware(request)` runs first on every non-`/search` request; for `pathname.startsWith('/auth/')` the auth0Response returns unchanged and an anon cookie is NOT stamped (the SDK is mid-handshake — stamping during a callback would race the session cookie). The trailing slash in `'/auth/'` is load-bearing: a regression to `'/auth'` (no slash) would skip cookie issuance on `/authentic`, `/author/*`, `/auth-status`, etc. — paths that share the prefix but are NOT auth routes; (3) **anon cookie issuance with security attributes** (`src/middleware.ts:43-58`) — when `isValidAnonId(existing)` fails (missing, empty, malformed UUID), mint a fresh UUID v4 and stamp with `httpOnly: true` (XSS containment — JS cannot exfiltrate), `sameSite: 'lax'` (CSRF defense), `secure: NODE_ENV === 'production'` (no plaintext leak in prod, but local http dev still works), `path: '/'`, `maxAge: ANON_COOKIE_MAX_AGE_SEC` (400-day Chrome clamp). A regression dropping `httpOnly` would let XSS exfiltrate the session-binding identifier; dropping `secure` in prod would expose the cookie over plaintext MITM; widening `sameSite` to `none` would enable CSRF; flipping `secure` to always-true would break local http dev. `config.matcher` exclusion pattern (`_next/static|_next/image|favicon\.ico|.*\.svg$|.*\.png$|.*\.ico$|.*\.json$|.*\.txt$`) — a regression on the matcher would either run Auth0 + anon-cookie logic on every JS chunk / image / favicon (perf hit + stale Set-Cookie on every asset), or skip a real page route. `apps/e2e/tests/anon-vote.spec.ts` exercises the anon cookie indirectly (an anon vote round-trip walks through middleware), but only the happy path and only with the dev `secure: false`; the `/search` retirement, the `/auth/` passthrough discipline, the cookie-overwrite-on-invalid path, the security attributes (especially `httpOnly` + `secure: NODE_ENV === 'production'`), and the matcher shape are all dark to e2e. - [x] [MED] `src/app/api/mod/action/route.ts` ships without a colocated test — the **last untested API route** in the product and the next-by-impact route-handler test gap after #131 pinned `/api/auth/me`, #132 pinned `/api/internal/recompute`, #134 pinned `/api/vote`, #135 pinned `/api/comment`, #136 pinned `/api/comments`, #137 pinned `/api/ranking/[show]`, and #140 pinned `/api/flag`. `/api/mod/action` is the RBAC-gated moderation entry point a mod hits from `/mod` to approve / hide / remove / unhide / dismiss-flag a comment — every state transition a comment can make under moderation flows through this single POST and writes a `mod_actions` audit-log row. `apps/e2e/tests/mod-gate.spec.ts` walks two cases of the route (anon caller → `401 auth_required`; authed-but-not-mod → `403 not_a_mod`), but the route's full branch tree is dark to a hermetic walk because the hermetic mint-cookie user is **not** a mod (no `mod:read` in the Auth0 permissions claim) — the entire success path and every defense-in-depth contract are untestable via e2e: (1) **body validation (Zod)** — `commentId` UUID, `action` enum (5 values: `approve`/`hide`/`remove`/`unhide`/`dismiss_flag`), optional `note` (≤ 500 chars); malformed shapes each return `400 invalid_body`; the parse gate runs *before* session resolution; (2) **happy-path RBAC pass + RPC invocation** — for a real mod the route lazily `upsertUser`s + `claimAnonSession`s and invokes `modAction({sessionId, commentId, action, note})` with `note: parsed.note ?? null` (the route always passes a string|null, never `undefined`); (3) **RBAC gate (`isMod`)** — the route reads the live Auth0 permissions claim and 403s an authed caller without `mod:read`; the claim-shape normalization (array form *and* CSV-string form per `readPermissions`) must both work because Auth0 emits either depending on dashboard config; the not-a-mod branch returns *before* `upsertUser`/`claimAnonSession` so the route never half-claims a session for a user who failed the gate; (4) **defense-in-depth RPC error mapping** — the `mod_action()` RPC double-checks `users.is_mod` on the DB side, so `42501` from the RPC maps to **`403 not_a_mod`** (the Auth0 claim said yes, but the DB said no — distinct from `/api/flag`/`/api/comment` where `42501` maps to `401`), `22023 → 400 invalid_input`, anything else → `500 rpc_failed`; (5) **handleFromSession** falls through `nickname` (strip leading `@+`, lowercase) → email-localpart (lowercase) → sub-sanitized (`[^a-z0-9-]→-`, slice 32, lowercase) → "user", same multi-source fallback `/api/flag` and `/api/comment` use because magic-link sessions don't always carry a `nickname`; (6) **anon-cookie pass-through** — the resolved anon id is passed to `claimAnonSession` so prior anon activity is re-attributed; an invalid / absent cookie resolves to `anonId: null` and the action still ships; (7) **camelCase success shape** — the response echoes `{ok, status, actionId}` where `status` is `result.newStatus` (renamed from snake_case → camelCase by the mod helper, then renamed again by the route to drop the `new` prefix) and `actionId` is `Number(result.actionId)`; a regression returning the RPC's raw `new_status`/`action_id` shape, or spreading the helper result (`...result`), would silently break the `/mod` queue client's optimistic update; (8) **route contract** — `runtime === 'nodejs'`, `dynamic === 'force-dynamic'`. A regression in any of these branches passes the hermetic e2e suite — the e2e literally cannot test them — but would either let a non-mod approve/remove comments, drop the audit-log id, mis-derive the user handle, or break the `/mod` queue client. - [x] [MED] `src/app/api/ranking/[show]/route.ts` ships without a colocated test — the next-by-impact route-handler test gap after #131 pinned `/api/auth/me`, #132 pinned `/api/internal/recompute`, #134 pinned `/api/vote`, #135 pinned `/api/comment`, and #136 pinned `/api/comments`. `/api/ranking/[show]` is the contracted public read aggregate from the locked URL contract (`bearings.md` / `spec.md`: "GET /api/ranking/[show] — cached aggregate, served via ISR") and the only place the route returns the live community ranking shape consumed off the show page's polled client effect; phase 35's "vote → refresh shows true persisted net" acceptance criterion makes the route a regression-bearing surface for the three user-reported vote bugs it closed. `apps/e2e/tests/ranking-api.spec.ts` walks the route, but a hermetic e2e walk only ever drives the happy path against the live `getCommunityRanking` (canon-mirror fallback when the seed votes are absent), so the route's own four contracts are dark to it: (1) **the entry-shape transformation** — the route projects each `CommunityRankRow` to a *public* shape `{rank, seasonNumber, seasonSlug, title, tag, score, approval, voteCount, trend}` that drops the full internal `Season` object (a regression that spread `...e.season` or returned the row verbatim would leak internal frontmatter — `body_md`, `lede`, `pull`, `canonical_position`, every editorial draft field — to every show-page poll); (2) **the top-level response envelope** — `{ok, show, source, votersThisWeek, lastRecomputeAt, version, generatedAt}` keys; a regression that dropped `source` or `version` would break the client's trend / canon-mirror gating; `generatedAt` is a round-trippable ISO string; (3) **the 404 unknown-show branch** — `getShow(slug) → null` short-circuits to `{ok:false,error:'unknown_show'}` with `getCommunityRanking` *never* reached (the validation gate runs before the DB read); (4) **the loader pass-through** — `getCommunityRanking(show, seasons, canon)` is called with the *resolved* show plus its `getAllSeasons(show.slug)` + `getCanon(show.slug)` outputs verbatim (a regression that passed the URL slug instead of the resolved `show` would invalidate the canon-mirror fallback's tag derivation); and (5) **the `dynamic = 'force-dynamic'` contract** — a static bake would freeze one show's ranking into the route at build time and serve stale data on every poll, reintroducing exactly the staleness bug the route header explains the design rejected ISR caching to avoid; the next-15-route async-params await is also load-bearing under Next.js 15. A regression in any of these branches passes a hermetic e2e walk but would either leak internal season frontmatter to every public viewer, freeze the ranking, or 500 instead of 404'ing an unknown slug. - [x] [MED] `src/app/api/comment/route.ts` ships without a colocated test — the next-by-impact route-handler test gap after #131 pinned `/api/auth/me`, #132 pinned `/api/internal/recompute`, and #134 pinned `/api/vote`. `/api/comment` is the comment write path — every season page's `CommentInput` posts here — and it is the **only** path through which the OpenAI moderation pre-filter (`moderateComment`) runs before user copy hits the database. Spoiler discipline is P0 (CLAUDE.md "Five hard rules" + agents.md §7), so the verdict-pass-through contract is load-bearing. `apps/e2e/tests/comments.spec.ts` walks happy path + spoiler-blocked + flag flow, but the route's full branch tree is dark to it: (1) **body validation (Zod)** — `targetType` enum (`'season' | 'comment'`), `targetId` length bounds (1–128), `body` length bounds (1–4000), optional nullable UUID `parentId`; malformed shapes each return `400 invalid_body`; the parse gate runs *before* session resolution; (2) **auth gate** — `/api/comment` requires auth (unlike `/api/vote`), so an anon caller and a session with no `sub` each return `401 auth_required` with `postComment` never reached; the anon cookie regex + `isValidAnonId` UUID validation still run for genuine since the resolved anon id is passed to `claimAnonSession` so prior anon activity is re-attributed; an authed caller lazily `upsertUser`s + `claimAnonSession`s and posts as the **claimed** session id (not the raw anon id); (3) **handle derivation** — `handleFromSession` falls through `nickname` (strip leading `@+`, lowercase) → email-localpart (lowercase) → sub-sanitized (`[^a-z0-9-]→-`, slice 32, lowercase) → "user", distinct from `/api/vote`'s simpler nickname-only path because magic-link sessions don't always carry a `nickname`; (4) **verdict pass-through (spoiler discipline)** — `moderateComment(body)` runs exactly once on the parsed body string and *every* verdict field (`verdict`, `categories`, `confidence`, `reason`, `redacted_phrase`) passes through to `postComment` verbatim; a regression that drops `categories` or downgrades a `block` to `allow` would let spoilers slip past the moderation layer; (5) **verdict echo in success body** — the response echoes `verdict` alongside `id`, `status`, `count` so the client can render the held-for-review affordance when `status === 'pending'`; (6) **RPC error mapping** — `42501` (RLS) → `401 auth_required`, `23505` → `429 rate_limited` (new-account 5-comment hold + rate limit), `22023` → `400 invalid_input`, anything else → `500 rpc_failed`; (7) **auth-resolve failure** — a thrown `auth0.getSession()` maps to `500 auth_resolve_failed`; (8) **route contract** — `runtime === 'nodejs'`, `dynamic === 'force-dynamic'`. A regression in any of these branches passes a hermetic e2e walk but would either leak unmoderated text to the published thread, drop the auth gate, misroute a rate-limit to a 500, or mis-derive the user handle. Its `authorized(request)` guard is env-conditional: when `CRON_SECRET` is **set** (production — Vercel injects `Authorization: Bearer <CRON_SECRET>` on cron invocations) the header must equal `Bearer <CRON_SECRET>` *exactly*, else 401; when `CRON_SECRET` is **unset** (local dev + hermetic e2e) the route is **open** so the harness can seed a snapshot in-band. `apps/e2e/tests/ranking-api.spec.ts` exercises the route, but the hermetic e2e harness runs with `CRON_SECRET` unset — so e2e only ever walks the *open* branch. The production security branch (`!secret` false → exact-bearer compare → 401 on mismatch) is dark to every test: a regression inverting `if (!secret) return true`, dropping the bearer comparison, or loosening it to a case-insensitive / prefix match would let any unauthenticated caller force a service-role recompute in production and slip past the whole verify gate. The `?show=` param scoping (`p_show: null` when absent/empty), the `rowsWritten` numeric coercion, the RPC-error → 500 mapping, and GET/POST parity were also unpinned. - [x] [HIGH] season-page vote UX leaks Bayesian-prior internals — optimistic update shows `0.2`/`-0.55` blips before settling, "0.2 votes" on first visit, no voted/unvoting affordance, no graceful load-in, negative-direction phrasing is confusing (#64) (category: bug, source: triage, score: 3.2) — RESOLVED this commit: root cause was VotePair displaying the weighted aggregate `SUM(value*weight)` (a fractional ranking signal) as "net votes". Migration `20260518000001_vote_raw_count.sql` adds `raw_count = SUM(value)` to `cast_vote`/`read_vote`; the `/api/vote` route now sends the clean integer net to the client (weighted value stays internal). VotePair gains `aria-pressed` + persistent `.voted` tint + "click to undo" labels (clear voted/unvoting state), and a `data-hydrated` opacity fade so the number doesn't pop `0 → <X>`. Optimistic ±1 now reconciles exactly against the integer server delta — no more blips. Unit + e2e green. GitHub #64 closed by this commit.
